FINANCIAL_NNP STATEMENTS_NNS 1_CD ACCOUNTING_NNP POLICIES_NNPS The_DT financial_JJ statements_NNS have_VBP been_VBN prepared_VBN in_IN accordance_NN with_IN UK_NNP law_NN and_CC applicable_JJ The_DT principal_JJ accounting_NN policies_NNS are_VBP set_VBN out_RP below_IN :_: 1.1_CD ACCOUNTING_NNP CONVENTION_NNPS AND_CC BASIS_NNPS OF_IN CONSOLIDATION_NNP The_NNP consolidated_JJ financial_JJ statements_NNS are_VBP prepared_VBN under_IN the_DT historical_JJ cost_NN convention_NN ._.
The_DT consolidated_JJ financial_JJ statements_NNS incorporate_VBP the_DT financial_JJ statements_NNS of_IN the_DT Company_NN and_CC all_DT of_IN its_PRP$ subsidiaries_NNS and_CC associated_VBN undertakings_NNS ._.
The_DT results_NNS of_IN subsidiaries_NNS acquired_VBN are_VBP included_VBN from_IN the_DT date_NN on_IN which_WDT control_NN passes_VBZ ._.
The_DT net_JJ assets_NNS of_IN subsidiaries_NNS acquired_VBN are_VBP recorded_VBN at_IN their_PRP$ fair_JJ values_NNS ,_, reflecting_VBG their_PRP$ condition_NN at_IN that_DT date_NN ._.
The_DT results_NNS of_IN subsidiaries_NNS disposed_VBN of_IN are_VBP included_VBN up_RP to_TO the_DT effective_JJ date_NN of_IN disposal_NN ._.
Associated_NNP undertakings_NNS are_VBP accounted_VBN for_IN using_VBG the_DT equity_NN method_NN of_IN accounting_NN ._.
Accounting_NNP policies_NNS have_VBP been_VBN consistently_RB applied_VBN throughout_IN the_DT current_JJ and_CC preceding_JJ periods_NNS with_IN the_DT exception_NN of_IN the_DT changes_NNS caused_VBN by_IN the_DT implementation_NN of_IN Amendment_NNP to_TO FRS_NNP 5_CD Reporting_NNP the_DT substance_NN of_IN transactions_NNS :_: Revenue_NN recognition_NN Application_NNP Note_NN G_NNP and_CC the_DT adoption_NN of_IN Urgent_NNP Issues_NNP Task_NNP Force_NNP Abstract_NNP 38_CD Accounting_NN for_IN ESOP_NNP Trusts_NNPS UITF_NNP 38_CD which_WDT are_VBP further_JJ discussed_VBN below_IN ._.
1.2_CD CHANGE_NNP IN_IN ACCOUNTING_NNP POLICY_NNP AND_CC PRESENTATION_NNPS OF_IN FINANCIAL_NNP INFORMATION_NNP Application_NNP Note_VB G_NNP requires_VBZ the_DT seller_NN to_TO recognize_VB as_IN revenue_NN the_DT fair_JJ value_NN of_IN the_DT sellers_NNS right_RB to_TO consideration_NN through_IN performance_NN of_IN its_PRP$ contractual_JJ obligations_NNS ._.
Accordingly_RB ,_, turnover_NN in_IN respect_NN of_IN extended_JJ warranties_NNS and_CC service_NN contracts_NNS is_VBZ recognized_VBN over_IN the_DT life_NN of_IN the_DT agreement_NN on_IN performance_NN of_IN the_DT contractual_JJ obligations_NNS to_TO the_DT customer_NN ._.

Revenues_NNS earned_VBD from_IN extended_VBN warranties_NNS and_CC service_NN contracts_NNS were_VBD previously_RB included_VBN in_IN turnover_NN in_IN the_DT period_NN in_IN which_WDT they_PRP were_VBD sold_VBN with_IN full_JJ provision_NN for_IN liabilities_NNS for_IN repair_NN costs_NNS which_WDT the_DT Group_NNP had_VBD assumed_VBN under_IN these_DT contracts_NNS ._.
This_DT change_NN has_VBZ been_VBN accounted_VBN for_IN as_IN a_DT prior_JJ period_NN adjustment_NN and_CC previously_RB reported_VBN figures_NNS have_VBP been_VBN restated_VBN accordingly_RB ._.
The_DT financial_JJ effects_NNS on_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN and_CC balance_NN sheet_NN are_VBP set_VBN out_RP in_IN note_NN 33_CD ._.
UITF_NNP 38_CD supersedes_NNS UITF_NNP 13_CD and_CC amends_VBZ UITF_NNP 17_CD and_CC requires_VBZ own_JJ shares_NNS held_VBN through_IN an_DT employee_NN share_NN ownership_NN plan_NN trust_NN to_TO be_VB deducted_VBN in_IN arriving_VBG at_IN shareholders_NNS funds_NNS and_CC amends_VBZ the_DT requirements_NNS of_IN UITF_NNP 17_CD concerning_VBG the_DT recognition_NN of_IN the_DT cost_NN of_IN awards_NNS of_IN shares_NNS to_TO employees_NNS ._.
The_DT financial_JJ effects_NNS are_VBP set_VBN out_RP in_IN note_NN 33_CD ._.
1.3_CD TURNOVER_NNP Turnover_NN comprises_VBZ sales_NNS of_IN goods_NNS and_CC services_NNS excluding_VBG sales_NNS taxes_NNS ._.

1.4_CD OPERATING_NNP LEASES_NNP Rentals_NNPS payable_JJ under_IN property_NN leases_NNS are_VBP charged_VBN to_TO the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN in_IN equal_JJ instalments_NNS up_IN to_TO each_DT market_NN rent_NN review_NN date_NN throughout_IN the_DT lease_NN term_NN ._.

1.5_CD TRANSLATION_NNP OF_IN FOREIGN_NNP CURRENCIES_NNPS The_DT results_NNS of_IN overseas_JJ subsidiary_NN undertakings_NNS are_VBP translated_VBN into_IN sterling_NN at_IN the_DT average_JJ rates_NNS of_IN exchange_NN during_IN the_DT period_NN ._.
